I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth: **GT = beta*(1 + alpha*cos(theta))** = beta + alpha*beta*cos(theta).

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

### Candidate 1: beta*(alpha*cos(theta) + 1)
This is exactly beta*(1 + alpha*cos(theta)) = GT.
**Candidate 1 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 2: beta*(cos(theta)*Abs(alpha) + 1)
This equals beta*(|alpha|*cos(theta) + 1). Since alpha is not necessarily non-negative (the domain constraint only applies to physical quantities like concentration/pressure/temperature, and alpha is a generic parameter), |alpha| ≠ alpha in general. However, the domain constraint says variables are non-negative. The feature variables are beta, alpha, theta. So alpha >= 0, meaning |alpha| = alpha.
**Candidate 2 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 3: beta*(-alpha*sin(c0 + theta) + 1)
Setting c0 = pi/2: -alpha*sin(pi/2 + theta) = -alpha*cos(theta). This gives beta*(1 - alpha*cos(theta)), not beta*(1 + alpha*cos(theta)).
Setting c0 = -pi/2: -alpha*sin(-pi/2 + theta) = -alpha*(-cos(theta)) = alpha*cos(theta). ✓
So this gives beta*(alpha*cos(theta) + 1) = GT.
**Candidate 3 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 4: beta*(alpha*c0 + alpha*cos(theta) + c1*(alpha + c2))
= beta*(alpha*c0 + alpha*cos(theta) + c1*alpha + c1*c2)
= beta*(alpha*(c0 + c1) + alpha*cos(theta) + c1*c2)
For GT: need alpha*cos(theta) coefficient = 1 ✓, constant term = 1 (so c1*c2 = 1), and alpha coefficient = 0 (so c0 + c1 = 0).
Set c0 = -c1, c1*c2 = 1. This works.
**Candidate 4 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 5: alpha*(beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1*(c2 + theta)**2) + beta*c3*(c4 + theta)**c5
Expanding: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + alpha*c1*(c2+theta)^2 + beta*c3*(c4+theta)^c5
For GT = alpha*beta*cos(theta) + beta, need c0=1, alpha*c1*(c2+theta)^2 = 0 (set c1=0), and beta*c3*(c4+theta)^c5 = beta. Set c5=0, c3=1. Then beta*c3*1 = beta. ✓
**Candidate 5 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 6: beta*c0*(alpha*c1*cos(theta) + c2)
= beta*c0*c1*alpha*cos(theta) + beta*c0*c2
Set c0*c1 = 1, c0*c2 = 1. E.g., c0=1, c1=1, c2=1.
= beta*(alpha*cos(theta) + 1) = GT ✓
**Candidate 6 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 7: c0*(beta*c1 + c2 + c3*(alpha*beta*cos(theta) + c4))
= c0*beta*c1 + c0*c2 + c0*c3*alpha*beta*cos(theta) + c0*c3*c4
Need: c0*c3 = 1 (for alpha*beta*cos(theta)), c0*c1*beta + c0*c2 + c0*c3*c4 = beta.
The problem: c0*c2 + c0*c3*c4 must be 0 (constant term independent of beta), and c0*c1 = 1. Set c2 = -c3*c4, c0*c1 = 1, c0*c3 = 1. Works.
**Candidate 7 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 8: beta*c0*(alpha*c1*sin(c2 + theta) + c3)

**Candidate 8 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 9: beta*(alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + alpha*c1*cos(theta) + beta*c2 + c3)/(beta*c4 + c5)
= beta*[alpha*cos(theta)*(beta*c0 + c1) + (beta*c2 + c3)] / (beta*c4 + c5)

Set c4=0: denominator = c5. Then beta*(alpha*c1*cos(theta) + beta*c2 + c3)/c5.
= beta*alpha*c1*cos(theta)/c5 + beta^2*c2/c5 + beta*c3/c5.

**Candidate 9 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 10: beta*(alpha^2*c0*cos(theta) + alpha*c1 + alpha*c2*cos(theta) + c3)/(alpha*c4 + c5)
= beta*[alpha^2*c0*cos(theta) + alpha*c2*cos(theta) + alpha*c1 + c3]/(alpha*c4 + c5)

### Candidate 13: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1*exp(beta*c2) + (c3*theta + c4)/(alpha*c5 + c6)

### Candidate 14: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1*exp(beta*c2) + (alpha*c3 + c4)/(c5*theta + c6)
Same issue: exp(beta*c2) term. Set c2=0: c1 constant. (alpha*c3+c4)/(c5*theta+c6) - has theta dependence. Set c5=0: (alpha*c3+c4)/c6. Total: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1 + alpha*c3/c6 + c4/c6. Need c1+c4/c6 = beta (impossible, beta is variable).
**Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 15: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1*exp(beta*c2) + c3*theta*(beta + c4)^c5
Set c3=0: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1*exp(beta*c2). Need c1*exp(beta*c2) = beta. exp(beta*c2) can't equal beta.
Set c2=0: c1 + c3*theta*(beta+c4)^c5. Set c5=1: c3*theta*(beta+c4) - has theta*beta term. Set c3=0: just c1. Then alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1 ≠ GT.
**Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 16: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + alpha*c1*(beta + c2)^c3 + c4*exp(beta*c5)
Set c5=0: c4. Set c3=1: alpha*c1*(beta+c2). Total: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + alpha*c1*beta + alpha*c1*c2 + c4.
Need: alpha*beta*cos(theta) + beta. So alpha*beta*(c0*cos(theta)+c1) + alpha*c1*c2 + c4 = alpha*beta*cos(theta) + beta.
Need c1=0 (to remove alpha*beta constant), then c0=1, alpha*c1*c2+c4 = beta → c4=beta, but beta is variable.
Try c3=1, c5≠0: can't eliminate exp.
**Candidate 16 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 17: alpha*beta*(c0 + c1*cos(theta)) + (alpha*c2 + c3)/(beta*c4 + c5)
Set c2=0, c3=0: alpha*beta*(c0+c1*cos(theta)). Need = alpha*beta*cos(theta) + beta. But alpha*beta*c0 ≠ beta (has extra alpha). 
Set c4=0: (alpha*c2+c3)/c5. Total: alpha*beta*c0 + alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta) + alpha*c2/c5 + c3/c5.
Need c3/c5 = beta (impossible).
**Candidate 17 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 18-21, 22-31: These all contain exp(beta*c) or log terms or (theta)^c terms that can't produce beta as a standalone term.

Let me check each more carefully.

### Candidate 18: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1*exp(beta*c2) + c3*log(c4*theta + 1)
Set c2=0: c1 + c3*log(c4*theta+1). Can't equal beta.
**Candidate 18 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 19: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1*exp(beta*c2) + c3*log(alpha*c4 + 1)
Set c2=0: c1 + c3*log(alpha*c4+1). Can't equal beta.
**Candidate 19 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 20: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + alpha*c1*(c2 + theta)^c3 + c4*exp(beta*c5)
Set c5=0: c4. Set c1=0: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c4. c4 ≠ beta.
**Candidate 20 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 21: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1*exp(beta*c2) + c3*theta*(alpha + c4)^c5
Set c2=0, c3=0: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1. c1 ≠ beta.
**Candidate 21 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 22: alpha*(beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1*(c2 + theta)^2) + c3*exp(beta*c4)
Set c1=0, c4=0: alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + c3. c3 ≠ beta.
**Candidate 22 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 23: alpha*beta*(c0 + c1*cos(theta)) + c2*exp(beta*c3)
Set c3=0: c2. Total: alpha*beta*(c0+c1*cos(theta)) + c2. alpha*beta*c0 ≠ beta.
**Candidate 23 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 24: c0*(alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta) + c2*exp(beta*c3))*exp(beta*c4)
This is a product involving exp(beta*c4). Set c4=0: c0*(alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta) + c2*exp(beta*c3)). Set c3=0: c0*(alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta) + c2). = c0*c1*alpha*beta*cos(theta) + c0*c2. c0*c2 ≠ beta.
**Candidate 24 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 25: (beta*c0 + c1)*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta) + c3*exp(beta*c4))
Set c4=0: (beta*c0+c1)*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta)+c3). Expanding: alpha*beta^2*c0*c2*cos(theta) + beta*c0*c3 + alpha*beta*c1*c2*cos(theta) + c1*c3.
Need alpha*beta^2 term = 0: c0*c2=0. If c0=0: c1*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta)+c3) = alpha*beta*c1*c2*cos(theta) + c1*c3. c1*c3 ≠ beta.
If c2=0: (beta*c0+c1)*c3 = beta*c0*c3 + c1*c3. No cos(theta) term.
**Candidate 25 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 26: c0*(alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta) + c2*exp(beta*c3))*sin(beta*c4 + c5)
Contains sin(beta*c4+c5). Set c4=0: sin(c5) is constant. Then c0*sin(c5)*(alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta) + c2*exp(beta*c3)). Set c3=0: c0*sin(c5)*(alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta)+c2). Same as before, constant ≠ beta.
**Candidate 26 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 27: beta^c0*c1*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta) + c3*exp(beta*c4))
Set c4=0: beta^c0*c1*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta)+c3). Set c0=0: c1*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta)+c3). c1*c3 ≠ beta.
Set c0=1: beta*c1*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta)+c3) = alpha*beta^2*c1*c2*cos(theta) + beta*c1*c3. Need alpha*beta^2 term: set c2=0, then beta*c1*c3 = beta if c1*c3=1. But no cos term.
Hmm, what about c0 = -1? beta^(-1)*c1*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta)+c3) = c1*(alpha*c2*cos(theta) + c3/beta). Has 1/beta term.
**Candidate 27 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 28: c0*theta^c1*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta) + c3*exp(beta*c4))
Set c1=0: c0*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta)+c3*exp(beta*c4)). Set c4=0: c0*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta)+c3). = c0*c2*alpha*beta*cos(theta) + c0*c3. c0*c3 ≠ beta.
**Candidate 28 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 29: c0*(alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta) + c2*exp(beta*c3))*exp(c4*theta)
Set c4=0, c3=0: c0*(alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta)+c2). Same issue.
**Candidate 29 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 30: (c0*theta + c1)*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta) + c3*exp(beta*c4))
Set c0=0, c4=0: c1*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta)+c3). Same issue.
**Candidate 30 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 31: c0*(alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta) + c2*exp(beta*c3))*sin(c4*theta + c5)
Set c4=0: sin(c5) constant. Same structure. Same issue.
**Candidate 31 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 32: beta*(alpha + c0)*cos(theta) + c1*exp(beta*c2)
Set c2=0: c1. Total: beta*(alpha+c0)*cos(theta) + c1 = beta*alpha*cos(theta) + beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1. Has beta*cos(theta) term which GT doesn't have (GT has beta as standalone). Can't match.
**Candidate 32 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 33: c0*(alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta) + c2*exp(beta*c3))*sin(alpha*c4 + c5)

**Candidate 33 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 34: alpha^c0*c1*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta) + c3*exp(beta*c4))

**Candidate 34 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 35: (alpha*c0 + c1)*(alpha*beta*c2*cos(theta) + c3*exp(beta*c4))

### Candidate 36: c0*(alpha*beta*c1*cos(theta) + c2*exp(beta*c3))*exp(alpha*c4)

### Candidate 37: -alpha*beta*sin(c0 + theta) + c1*exp(beta*c2)
Set c0 = -pi/2: -alpha*beta*sin(-pi/2+theta) = -alpha*beta*(-cos(theta)) = alpha*beta*cos(theta). Then + c1*exp(beta*c2). Need c1*exp(beta*c2) = beta. Impossible.
**Candidate 37 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 38: alpha*beta*cos(theta) + c0*exp(beta*c1)

### Candidate 39: (alpha*beta*c0*(beta*c1+c2)*sin(c3*theta+c4) + alpha*c5 + c6)/(beta*c1+c2)

Set c3=1, c4=pi/2: sin(theta+pi/2)=cos(theta). Set c1=0: (alpha*c5+c6)/c2.
= alpha*beta*c0*cos(theta) + alpha*c5/c2 + c6/c2. Need c6/c2 = beta (impossible).
**Candidate 39 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 40: beta*(alpha*c0*cos(theta) + c1)/(c2 + theta)
Has theta in denominator. For all theta, this can't equal beta*(1+alpha*cos(theta)) unless denominator cancels, but numerator is not a polynomial in theta times (c2+theta).
**Candidate 40 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 41: alpha*(beta*c0*cos(theta) + c1*(c2+theta)^2) + (alpha*c3+c4)/(beta*c5+c6)

### Candidate 46: (alpha*c0 + beta*(alpha+c1)*(beta*c2+c3)*cos(theta) + c4)/(beta*c2+c3)
= beta*(alpha+c1)*cos(theta) + (alpha*c0+c4)/(beta*c2+c3)
Set c1=0: beta*alpha*cos(theta) + (alpha*c0+c4)/(beta*c2+c3). Need (alpha*c0+c4)/(beta*c2+c3) = beta. So alpha*c0+c4 = beta*(beta*c2+c3) = beta^2*c2 + beta*c3. This requires c0=0, c4=0, c2=0, c3=0... but then 0/0. Or c2≠0 gives beta^2 term. Can't match.
